/*

WITH "b" AS (
    SELECT "N" || ', ' || 
            (CASE 
               WHEN "P" IS NULL THEN 'NULL' 
               ELSE "P"::text
           END) || ''
      AS "s"
    FROM "BST"
)
SELECT string_agg("s", CHR(10))
FROM "b";

*/

BST = {
  N:number, P:number

  1, 2
  3, 2
  5, 6
  7, 6
  2, 4
  6, 4
  4, 15
  8, 9
  10, 9
  12, 13
  14, 13
  9, 11
  13, 11
  11, 15
  15, NULL
}

/*

    SELECT "ID" || ', "' || 
           "NAME" || '", "' || 
           "COUNTRYCODE" || '", "' ||         
           "DISTRICT" || '", ' || 
           "POPULATION" 
      AS "s"
    FROM "CITY"
)
SELECT string_agg("s", CHR(10))
FROM "r";

*/

WITH "r" AS (
    SELECT '' || 
           (CASE 
               WHEN "challenge_id" IS NULL THEN 'NULL' 
               ELSE "challenge_id"::text

               ELSE "hacker_id"::text
           END) || ', ' ||
					 (CASE 
               WHEN "difficulty_level" IS NULL THEN 'NULL' 
               ELSE "difficulty_level"::text
           END) || ''
      AS "s"
    FROM "Challenges"
)

FROM "r";

/*

WITH "r" AS (
    SELECT '' || 
           (CASE 
               WHEN "ID" IS NULL THEN 'NULL' 
               ELSE "ID"::text 
           END) || ', ' || 
           (CASE 
               WHEN "Name" IS NULL THEN 'NULL' 
               ELSE "Name"::text 
           END) || ', ' || 
           (CASE 
               WHEN "Marks" IS NULL THEN 'NULL' 
               ELSE "Marks"::text 
           END) || ''
      AS "s"
    FROM "STUDENTS"
)
SELECT string_agg("s", CHR(10))
FROM "r";

*/

/*

WITH "r" AS (
    SELECT '' || 
           (CASE 
               WHEN "A" IS NULL THEN 'NULL' 
               ELSE "A"::text 
           END) || ', ' || 
           (CASE 
               WHEN "B" IS NULL THEN 'NULL' 
               ELSE "B"::text 
           END) || ', ' || 
           (CASE 
               WHEN "C" IS NULL THEN 'NULL' 
               ELSE "C"::text 
           END) || ''
      AS "s"
    FROM "TRIANGLES"
)
SELECT string_agg("s", CHR(10))
FROM "r";

*/

TRIANGLES = {
	A:number, B:number, C:number

	10, 10, 10
  11, 11, 11
  30, 32, 30
  40, 40, 40
  20, 20, 21
  21, 21, 21
  20, 22, 21
  20, 20, 40
  20, 22, 21
  30, 32, 41
  50, 22, 51
  20, 12, 61
  20, 22, 50
  50, 52, 51
  80, 80, 80
}
